ACTOR PlasmaGunner1 : PlasmaGunner replaces PlasmaGunner
{
Species "Hell"
DamageFactor "Hell", 0.0
DropItem "BonusCrateDrop" 1
+DONTHARMSPECIES
MaxStepHeight 32
MaxDropOffHeight 32
Tag "\c[m5]Plasmagunner\c-"
States
{
  Death:
	ZMAY H 5
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("WeakCrateGiver",1)
	ZMAY I 5 A_Scream
	ZMAY J 5 A_Fall
	ZMAY K 5
	ZMAY L 0 A_SpawnItem("BodyCrash",0,0,0,0)
	ZMAY L -1
	Stop
  Missile:
	ZMAY E 15 A_FaceTarget
	ZMAY F 2 Bright A_CustomMissile("FasterZombiePlasmaBall", 30, 4, 0)
	ZMAY E 3 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(102,"Pause")
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpidRefire
	Goto Missile+1
  XDeath:
	ZMAY O 3
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("WeakCrateGiver",1)
	ZMAY P 3 A_XScream
	ZMAY Q 3 A_SpawnItemEx("GibbedGenerator",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128,0)
	ZMAY R 3 A_Fall
	ZMAY STU 3
	ZMAY V -1
	Stop
}
}

ACTOR FasterZombiePlasmaBall : ZombiePlasmaBall
{
Speed 55
FastSpeed 55
Decal HeatScorch
}

ACTOR RailGunner1 : RailGunner replaces RailGunner
{
Species "Hell"
DamageFactor "Hell", 0.0
DropItem "BonusCrateDrop" 1
+DONTHARMSPECIES
MaxStepHeight 32
MaxDropOffHeight 32
Tag "\c[t1]Railgunner\c-"
States
{
Missile:
        RPOS E 18 A_FaceTarget
		RPOS E 2
		TNT1 A 0 Bright //A_PlaySound("railgunner/chargedshot")
		TNT1 A 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("RailgunImpactRed",30)
        RPOS F 5 Bright A_CustomRailgun(Random(15,25),0,"Red",None,RGF_NOPIERCING,1,1,"HellBulletPuff",0,0,0,0,0.45,0,"NewRailgunTrailRed")
        RPOS E 40
		Goto See
Death:
        RPOS H 5
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("WeakCrateGiver",1)
        RPOS I 5 A_Scream
        RPOS J 5 A_Fall
        RPOS K 5 A_SpawnItem("BodyCrash",0,0,0,0)
        RPOS LM 5
        RPOS N -1
        Stop
XDeath:
        ZMAY O 3
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("WeakCrateGiver",1)
        ZMAY P 3 A_XScream
        ZMAY Q 3 A_SpawnItemEx("GibbedGenerator",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128,0)
        ZMAY R 3 A_Fall
        ZMAY STU 3
        ZMAY V -1
        Stop
}
}

ACTOR RocketZombie1 : RocketZombie replaces RocketZombie
{
Species "Hell"
DamageFactor "Hell", 0.0
DropItem "BonusCrateDrop" 1
+DONTHARMSPECIES
+QUICKTORETALIATE
MaxStepHeight 32
MaxDropOffHeight 32
Tag "\ccRocket Zombie\c-"
States
{
  Spawn:
    MPO2 A 10 A_Look
	MPOI A 10 A_Look
    Loop
  See:
    MPO2 AABB 3 A_Chase
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("FootStep",0,0,0,0)
    MPO2 CCDD 3 A_Chase
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("FootStep",0,0,0,0)
    Loop
  Missile:
    MPO2 E 14 A_FaceTarget
    MPO2 F 6 Bright A_CustomMissile("UpdatedDemonRocket", 30, 0, 0)
	MPO2 E 20 A_PlaySound("rocket/drumspin")
    Goto See
  Pain:
    MPO2 G 6 A_Pain
    Goto See
  Death:
    MPO2 H 5 A_Scream
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("WeakCrateGiver",1)
    MPO2 I 5 A_Fall
    MPO2 J 5 A_SpawnItem("BodyCrash",0,0,0,0)
    MPO2 K 5
    MPO2 L -1
    Stop
  XDeath:
    MPO2 M 3
    MPO2 N 3 A_XScream
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("WeakCrateGiver",1)
    MPO2 O 3 A_SpawnItemEx("GibbedGenerator",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128,0)
    MPO2 P 3 A_Fall
    MPO2 QRST 3
    MPO2 U -1
    Stop
}
}

ACTOR SuperShotgunZombie1 : SuperShotgunZombie replaces SuperShotgunZombie
{
Species "Hell"
DamageFactor "Hell", 0.0
DropItem "BonusCrateDrop" 1
+DONTHARMSPECIES
MaxStepHeight 32
MaxDropOffHeight 32
Tag "\ccDouble Shotgunner\c-"
Decal BulletChip
States
{
Missile:
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SSGZombieToken",2,"Reload")
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(275,"Double")
Normal:
    UDM2 E 15 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/ssgsingleshot")
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("SSGZombieToken",1)
	TNT1 AAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("MonsterTracer2",Random(28,34),0,Random(6,-6),0)
    UDM2 F 4 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(22.5,0,3,Random(1,5)*3,"HellBulletPuff")
    UDM2 E 8 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SSGZombieToken",2,"Reload")
	Goto See
Double:
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SSGZombieToken",1,"Normal")
    UDM2 E 15 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/sshotf")
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("SSGZombieToken",2)
	TNT1 AAAAAAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("MonsterTracer2",Random(28,34),0,Random(6,-6),0)
    UDM2 F 5 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(13.8,9.6,10,Random(1,4)*3,"HellBulletPuff")
    UDM2 E 15 A_FaceTarget
	Goto Reload
Death:
    UDM2 H 5
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("WeakCrateGiver",1)
    UDM2 I 5 A_Scream
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("BodyCrash",0,0,0,0)
    UDM2 J 5 A_Fall
    UDM2 K 5
    UDM2 L -1
    Stop
XDeath:
    ASGZ O 3 A_SpawnItemEx("GibbedGenerator",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("WeakCrateGiver",1)
    ASGZ P 3 A_XScream
    ASGZ R 3 A_Fall
    ASGZ STUV 3
    ASGZ W -1
    Stop
    }
}

ACTOR Hexa-ShotgunZombie1 : Hexa-ShotgunZombie replaces Hexa-ShotgunZombie
{
Species "Hell"
DamageFactor "Hell", 0.0
DropItem "BonusCrateDrop" 1
+DONTHARMSPECIES
+QUICKTORETALIATE
MaxStepHeight 32
MaxDropOffHeight 32
var int user_script;
Tag "\ccHexa Shotgunner\c-"
Decal BulletChip
States
{
Spawn:
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_script == 1,4)
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(ACS_ExecuteWithResult(3708,0,0,0) == TRUE,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Changeflag("NOPAIN",1)
    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_script",1)
	Goto Super::Spawn
Missile:
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Hexa-ZombieToken",3,"Reload")
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(325,"Hexa")
Normal:
    HSZM E 15 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/qsgdoublefire")
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Hexa-ZombieToken",1)
	TNT1 AAAAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("MonsterTracer2",Random(28,34),0,Random(6,-6),0)
    HSZM F 5 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(13.8,9.6,10,Random(1,4)*3,"HellBulletPuff")
    HSZM E 15 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Hexa-ZombieToken",3,"Reload")
	Goto See
Hexa:
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Hexa-ZombieToken",1,"Normal")
    HSZM E 15 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/hsgfire")
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Hexa-ZombieToken",3)
	TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("MonsterTracer2",Random(28,34),0,Random(6,-6),0)
    HSZM F 5 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(15.4,10.6,78,Random(1,4)*3,"HellBulletPuff")
    HSZM E 25 A_FaceTarget
	Goto Reload
Death:
    HSZM H 5 A_GiveToTarget("MediumCrateGiver",1)
    HSZM I 5 A_Scream
    HSZM J 5 A_Fall
    HSZM K 5 A_SpawnItem("BodyCrash",0,0,0,0)
    HSZM L -1
    Stop
XDeath:
    HSZM M 3 A_GiveToTarget("MediumCrateGiver",1)
    HSZM N 3 A_XScream
    HSZM O 3 A_SpawnItemEx("GibbedGenerator",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128,0)
	HSZM P 3 A_Fall
    HSZM HRST 3
    HSZM U -1
    Stop
    }
}

	SGCD E 1 A_GiveInventory("CommandoStrafing",1)

    SGCD L 5

{
Species "Hell"

DropItem "BonusCrateDrop" 1
+DONTHARMSPECIES
+QUICKTORETALIATE
MaxStepHeight 32
MaxDropOffHeight 32
var int user_script;
Tag "\ccMinigunner\c-"
Decal BulletChip
States
{
Spawn:

    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(ACS_ExecuteWithResult(3708,0,0,0) == TRUE,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Changeflag("NOPAIN",1)
    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_script",1)
	Goto Super::Spawn
  Missile:
    TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/mgunspinstart")
    CPS2 E 10 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("weapons/mgunspin","Voice")
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("MonsterTracer",Random(30,34),0,Random(5,-5),0)
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RifleCasing", 12, 6, 28, Random(2, 6), 0, Random(1, 3), Random(-80, -90), 128)
    CPS2 E 3 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(22.5,0,1,random(1,5)*3,"HellBulletPuff",0,CBAF_NORANDOM)

    LPOS R 3 A_Fall
    LPOS STUV 3
    LPOS W -1
    Stop
 }

ACTOR LegendaryAssaultCaptain1 : LegendaryAssaultCaptain replaces LegendaryAssaultCaptain
{
Species "Hell"
DamageFactor "Hell", 0.0
DamageFactor "BFGSplash", 0.5
DamageFactor "PDTBFG", 0.4
DamageFactor "PDTBFGTracer", 0.4
DamageFactor "MechStep", 0.0
DamageFactor "Pierce", 0.25
DamageFactor "MarinePierce", 0.25
DamageFactor "Kaboom", 0.2
DamageFactor "MarineKaboom", 0.2
DropItem "BonusCrateDrop" 1
+DONTHARMSPECIES
+NOTIMEFREEZE
+NOFEAR
-NOBLOCKMONST
MaxStepHeight 32
MaxDropOffHeight 32
var int user_script;
Tag "\c[z3]Legendary Assault Captain\c-"
AttackSound ""
Decal LegBulletChip
States
{
  Spawn:
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_script == 1,5)
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(ACS_ExecuteWithResult(3708,0,0,0) == TRUE,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Changeflag("NOPAIN",1)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Strong Monster Phase Setter",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_script",1)
	Goto Super::Spawn
  See:
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_script == 1,5)
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(ACS_ExecuteWithResult(3708,0,0,0) == TRUE,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Changeflag("NOPAIN",1)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Strong Monster Phase Setter",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_script",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetInvulnerable
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("ImStillAliveSomehow")
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	LASG AA 4 Bright A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	LASG BB 4 Bright A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("FootStep",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	LASG CC 4 Bright A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	LASG DD 4 Bright A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("FootStep",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,"Mine")
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,"Rush")
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,"DodgeLeft","DodgeRight")
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("IsAwakenedLegendaryMonster",1,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(30,"Teleport")
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,"Chase")
	Loop
  Chase:
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	LASG AA 1 Bright A_FastChase
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(1,"Heal")
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(130,"Dodge")
	LASG AA 1 Bright A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(130,"Dodge")
	LASG BB 1 Bright A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(130,"Dodge")
	LASG BB 1 Bright A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("FootStep",0,0,2,0,0,-20)
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(150,"Dodge")
	LASG CC 1 Bright A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(10,"Heal")
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(150,"Dodge")
	LASG CC 1 Bright A_FastChase
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(130,"Dodge")
	LASG DD 1 Bright A_FastChase
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(130,"Dodge")
	LASG DD 1 Bright A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("FootStep",0,0,2,0,0,-20)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(95,"Mine")
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("IsAwakenedLegendaryMonster",1,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(30,"Teleport")
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128,"Dodge")
	Loop
  Rush:
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("FootStep",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("LegASGZombieGhostA",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128)
	LASG A 1 Bright A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("LegASGZombieGhostA",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128)
	LASG A 1 Bright A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("LegASGZombieGhostB",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128)
	LASG B 1 Bright A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("LegASGZombieGhostB",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128)
	LASG B 1 Bright A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("FootStep",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("LegASGZombieGhostC",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128)
	LASG C 1 Bright A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("LegASGZombieGhostC",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128)
	LASG C 1 Bright A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("LegASGZombieGhostD",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128)
	LASG D 1 Bright A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("LegASGZombieGhostD",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128)
	LASG D 1 Bright A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("FootStep",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(85,"See")
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("IsAwakenedLegendaryMonster",1,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(30,"Teleport")
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	Loop
  Teleport:
	LASG E 1 Bright A_UnSetShootable
	TNT1 AAAA 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	LASG EEEEEEEEEE 1 A_FadeOut(0.1,0)       
	LASG E 2 
	TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_Wander
	TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_Wander
	LASG E 1 A_PlayWeaponSound("boss/teleport")
	TNT1 AAAA 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	LPOS EEEEEEEEEEE 1 A_FadeIn(0.1)
	LPOS E 1 Bright A_SetShootable
	Goto See
  Missile:
	TNT1 A 0 
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetShootable
	TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetInvulnerable
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetTranslucent(1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("ImStillAliveSomehow")
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(500,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,"Grenade")
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(48,"FloatingMine","LegQuad")
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,"Shotgun")
  Shotgun:
	LASG E 3 Bright A_GiveInventory("LegZombieStrafing",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("LegZombieStrafing",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	LASG E 4 Bright A_GiveInventory("LegZombieStrafing",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BlueShellCasing",-8,7,30,4,0,(0.1)*random(30,40),random(-80,-90),128)
	TNT1 AAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("LegendaryBlueTracer",random(28,34),0,random(6,-6),0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("Weapons/LegAutoShotgun")
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("IsAwakenedLegendaryMonster",1,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,5)
	TNT1 AAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("LegRevBall2",32,0,random(-3,3))				
	LASG F 2 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(16.5,7.5,7,random(2,10)*6,"HellBulletPuff")
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("LegZombieStrafing",1)
	LASG E 4 Bright A_GiveInventory("LegZombieStrafing",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(48,"See","Grenade","FloatingMine","LegQuad")
	TNT1 A 0 A_CPosRefire
	Goto Shotgun+1
  Mine:
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_minefield",0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(300,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfTargetInLos("Missile")
	LASG C 2 Bright A_GiveInventory("LegZombieStrafing",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_minefield",user_minefield+1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetAngle(random(0,360))
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("LACThrownMine1",32,0,0,2,15)
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("IsAwakenedLegendaryMonster",1,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,4)
	TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("LACThrownMine1",32,0,random(0,359),2,15)
	LASG EEEEEE 3 Bright A_GiveInventory("LegZombieStrafing",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_minefield >= 4,"See")
	LASG C 3 Bright A_GiveInventory("LegZombieStrafing",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,"See")
	LASG C 3 Bright A_GiveInventory("LegZombieStrafing",1)
	Goto Mine+1
  Grenade:
	TNT1 A 0 
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("IsAwakenedLegendaryMonster",1,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(78,"AwakenedGrenade")
	TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("LegendaryGrenade/Ready",0,1.0,0)
	LASG CCCCEEEE 3 Bright A_GiveInventory("LegZombieStrafing",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("LegendaryGrenade/Launch",0,1.0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("LACGrenade1",32,0,0,2,4)
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("IsAwakenedLegendaryMonster",1,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,3)
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("LACGrenade1",32,0,6,2,4)
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("LACGrenade1",32,0,-6,2,4)
	LASG EEEE 3 Bright A_GiveInventory("LegZombieStrafing",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_CPosRefire
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("IsAwakenedLegendaryMonster",1,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(78,"AwakenedGrenade")
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(156,"Dodge")
	Goto Grenade
  AwakenedGrenade:
	TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("LegendaryGrenade/Ready",0,1.0,0)
	LASG CCCCEEEE 3 Bright A_GiveInventory("LegZombieStrafing",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("LegendaryGrenade/Launch",0,1.0,0)

	TNT1 A 0 A_CPosRefire
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(156,"Dodge")
	Goto AwakenedGrenade
  LegQuad:
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetInvulnerable
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("lasgguy/sight")
	LASG E 1 Bright A_FaceTarget
	LASG EEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEE 3 Bright A_GiveInventory("LegZombieStrafing2",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("LegendaryQuadShotgun/Up")

	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,9)
	TNT1 AAAAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("LegRevBall",32,0,random(-6,6))
	TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("LegendaryBlueTracer",random(28,34),0,random(6,-6),0)
	LASG FFEEEEEEEEEEEEEEE 3 Bright A_GiveInventory("LegZombieStrafing",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,"FloatingMine")
	Goto See
  FloatingMine:
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetInvulnerable
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("lasgguy/sight")
	LASG E 1 Bright A_FaceTarget
	LASG EEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEE 3 Bright A_GiveInventory("LegZombieStrafing3",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("legendarycannon/charge")
	LASG EEEEE 3 Bright A_GiveInventory("LegZombieStrafing3",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/minebounce")
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("MineLauncher/Fire")
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("LegendaryAssaultCaptainFloatingMineProj",32,0,0)
	//TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("LegendaryAssaultCaptainFloatingMine",0,0,32,random(4,8),random(-2,2),0,32)
	LASG FFEE 3 Bright A_GiveInventory("LegZombieStrafing",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/minebounce")
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("MineLauncher/Fire")
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("LegendaryAssaultCaptainFloatingMineProj",32,0,0)
	LASG FFEE 3 Bright A_GiveInventory("LegZombieStrafing",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/minebounce")
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("MineLauncher/Fire")
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("LegendaryAssaultCaptainFloatingMineProj",32,0,0)
	LASG FFEE 3 Bright A_GiveInventory("LegZombieStrafing",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/minebounce")
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("MineLauncher/Fire")
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("LegendaryAssaultCaptainFloatingMineProj",32,0,0)
	LASG FFEE 3 Bright A_GiveInventory("LegZombieStrafing",1)
	LASG EE 4 Bright A_GiveInventory("LegZombieStrafing",1)
	Goto See
  Pain:
	//TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(20,"Protection")
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(20,"Dodge")
	LASG G 3 Bright
	LASG G 3 Bright A_Pain
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(40,"Dodge")
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(192,"Missile")
	Goto See
  Death:
	TNT1 A 0 A_StopSound(6)
	LASG H 5
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("EpicCrateGiver",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("PowerCrateGiver",1)
	TNT1 AAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("LACGrenade1",0,0,32,random(1,5),0,random(2,6),random(0,359))
	LASG I 5 A_Scream
	LASG J 5 A_Fall
	LASG J 5 A_SpawnItem("BodyCrash",0,0,0,0)
	LASG K 5
	LASG L -1
	Stop
  XDeath:
	TNT1 A 0 A_StopSound(6)
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("EpicCrateGiver",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("PowerCrateGiver",1)
	TNT1 AAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("LACGrenade1",0,0,32,random(1,5),0,random(2,6),random(0,359))
	LASG O 5 A_SpawnItemEx("BlueGibbedGenerator",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128,0)
	LASG P 5 A_XScream
	LASG Q 5 A_Fall
	LASG RSTUV 5
	LASG W -1
	Stop
}
}

ACTOR LegendaryStealthTrooper1 : LegendaryStealthTrooper replaces LegendaryStealthTrooper
{
Species "Hell"
DamageFactor "Hell", 0.0
DamageFactor "BFGSplash", 0.5

DamageFactor "PDTBFGTracer", 0.4

DamageFactor "Pierce", 0.25
DamageFactor "MarinePierce", 0.25
DamageFactor "Kaboom", 0.2

DropItem "BonusCrateDrop" 1
+DONTHARMSPECIES
+NOTIMEFREEZE
+NOFEAR
-NOBLOCKMONST
MaxStepHeight 32
MaxDropOffHeight 32
var int user_script;

Decal None
States
{

	TNT1 A 0 A_Changeflag("NOPAIN",1)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Strong Monster Phase Setter",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_script",1)
	Goto Super::Spawn
  See:

	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(ACS_ExecuteWithResult(3708,0,0,0) == TRUE,2)

	TNT1 A 0 A_Changeflag("NOPAIN",1)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Strong Monster Phase Setter",0,0,0,0)

	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("ImStillAliveSomehow")
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
    LCMD A 0 A_JumpIfTargetInLOS("Strafing")
    LCMD AA 3 Bright A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	LCMD BB 3 Bright A_Chase

    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LegendaryFootStep",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)	
    Loop
  Rush:
    LCMD A 0 A_JumpIfTargetInLOS("Strafing")
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LegendaryFootStep",0,0,0,0)

	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(80,"Phase")

    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LHellionSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)

	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("LegCommandoGhostC",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128)

  Phase:
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("phaseimp/teleport")
	LCMD E 2 A_FaceTarget

  SniperAttack:

	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("LegZombieStrafing2",1)

	LSOL B 0 A_FaceTarget
	LSOL B 4 Bright A_CustomMissile("LegSoulBall",20,0,random(-3,3))
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(88,"LegendarySparkProj")
	Goto See
  LegendarySparkProj:
   	LSOL BBB 3 Bright A_FaceTarget
	LSOL B 0 A_FaceTarget
	LSOL B 4 Bright A_CustomMissile("LegendarySparkProj",20,0,random(-3,3))

  Pain:

  Death:

    Stop
	}

ACTOR LegendaryRedeemer1 : LegendaryRedeemer replaces LegendaryRedeemer

States
{
  Spawn:
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_script == 1,5)
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(ACS_ExecuteWithResult(3708,0,0,0) == TRUE,2)

	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Strong Monster Phase Setter",0,0,0,0)
    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_script",1)
	Goto Super::Spawn
  See:

    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(ACS_ExecuteWithResult(3708,0,0,0) == TRUE,2)

	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Strong Monster Phase Setter",0,0,0,0)
    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_script",1)

	TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetInvulnerable
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("ImStillAliveSomehow")
	TNT1 AAA 0 A_SpawnItem("LRedeYSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
    LRED AAA 2 Bright A_Chase

	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(68,"Avoid","Rush","Teleport")
    Loop
  SeeSuicide:

    LRED A 3 Bright A_Chase("","Kamikaze")

  Teleport:

	LRED AAA 0 A_SpawnItem("LRedeYSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)

	LRED A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(2500,2)
	LRED A 0 A_Jump(256,6)
	LRED AAA 0 A_SpawnItem("LRedeYSmokeSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	LRED A 8
	LRED AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_Wander
    LRED A 1 A_PlayWeaponSound("boss/teleport")

	LRED AAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_FadeIn(0.1)
    LRED A 1 A_SetShootable
    Goto See
  Trap:

	TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_trap",0)

    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_trap",user_trap+3)

	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("LegRedTrap2",45,0,16,15,4)

ACTOR Exile1 : Exile replaces Exile
{
Species "Hell"

+DONTHARMSPECIES
MaxStepHeight 32

States
{
Death:
    VILE Q 6
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("MediumCrateGiver",1)
    VILE R 5 A_Scream
    VILE S 5 A_Fall
    VILE TUV 5
	VILE W 4 A_SpawnItem("BodyCrash",0,0,0,0)
    VILE XY 4
    VILE Z -1
    Stop
XDeath:
	VILX A 4
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("MediumCrateGiver",1)
	VILX B 3 A_XScream
	VILX C 3 A_SpawnItemEx("GibbedGenerator",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128,0)
	VILX D 3 A_Fall
	VILX E 3 A_SpawnItem("BodyCrash",0,0,0,0)
	VILX FG 3
	VILX H -1
	Stop
    }
}

ACTOR CerebralCardinal1 : CerebralCardinal replaces CerebralCardinal
{
Species "Hell"
DamageFactor "Hell", 0.0
DamageFactor "Legendary", 0.5
DamageFactor "BFGSplash", 0.25
DamageFactor "PDTBFG", 0.2
DamageFactor "PDTBFGTracer", 0.2
DamageFactor "MechStep", 0.0
DamageFactor "Pierce", 0.25
DamageFactor "MarinePierce", 0.25
DamageFactor "Kaboom", 0.2
DamageFactor "MarineKaboom", 0.2
DamageFactor 0.6
DropItem "BonusCrateDrop" 1
+DONTHARMSPECIES
-NOBLOCKMONST
+NOFEAR
+BRIGHT
RadiusDamageFactor 0.66
MaxStepHeight 32
MaxDropOffHeight 32
Health 15000
PainChance 2
Radius 65
var int user_script;
var int user_wait;
var int user_missile;
Tag "\c[w8]Cerebral Cardinal\c-"
States
{
  Spawn:
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_script == 1,7)
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(ACS_ExecuteWithResult(3708,0,0,0) == TRUE,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Changeflag("NOPAIN",1)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Strong Monster Phase Setter",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("CerebralSentientFireFollower",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_script",1)
	TNT1 A 0
	Goto Super::Spawn
  See:
	TNT1 A 0 
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_script == 1,7)
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(ACS_ExecuteWithResult(3708,0,0,0) == TRUE,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Changeflag("NOPAIN",1)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Strong Monster Phase Setter",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("CerebralSentientFireFollower",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_script",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetInvulnerable
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("ImStillAliveSomehow")
    ARCY A 0 A_SpawnItem("SentientFireSpawner",0,0,0,0)
    ARCY A 2 A_Chase
    TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(32,"Evade")	
    Loop
  Evade:
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128,"EvadeAlt")
	TNT1 A 0 ThrustThing(Angle*256/360+64,20,0,0)
	ARCY AAAAAAAA 2 A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_Stop
	Goto See
  EvadeAlt:
	TNT1 A 0 ThrustThing(Angle*256/360+192,20,0,0)
	ARCY AAAAAAAA 2 A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_Stop
	Goto See
  Missile:
	TNT1 A 0 
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetShootable
    TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetInvulnerable
    TNT1 A 0 A_SetTranslucent(1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("ImStillAliveSomehow")
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(16,"FusionNuke")
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(188,"CyberRockets","CyberHomingRockets","HeavyRocket","Railgun","BFG9K","BFG10K","MiniDTBFG","DTBFG10K","HellStormBFG10K","HellStormAltBFG10K","BFG12K","SuperLazer","Devastator","EradicationBFG","EradicationBFGAlt")
	TNT1 A 0
  Normal:
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(1500,1)
	Goto CyberHomingRockets
	ARCY AAA 2 A_FaceTarget
